<Author>Scohn
<Content>Great Small Hotel On Condado We just got back from staying at the At Wind Chimes Inn from June 15-23. This small hotel is an oasis in San Juan, with a staff that is among the most friendly and welcoming I have ever met. We came from Chicago with our 2 children (10 and 16) and the staff gave us a great rate on two rooms (one queen bed one with two double beds) for staying the whole 9 days there.The rooms are small but clean and comfortable. They certainly weren't fancy, but quite reasonable and the beds very comfortable. The original art in the rooms is also a very nice touch. The location was excellent. It was convenient to the beach (1/2 block from a great section of Condado beach which was never very crowded with great soft sand and warm and inviting water) as well as only a short walk to a 24 hour grocery store (we kept a small fridge in our room for fruit, water, and snacks - at a small additional fee). It also had excellent access to the highways and busses. We rented a car for a week of the trip, and although they were out of reserved parking spaces we usually could find a spot to park on one of the two blocks next to the hotel, and never felt any security problem parking there. The small pool was very calm and relaxing, and despite its small size was great for us as we were the only people using it on every occasion but one. They also have several small decks for lounging and some nice plants and a charming deck with a number of wind chimes. They also have a nice bar which also serves breakfast and lunch/dinner plates.But more than the nice rooms and charming and relaxing atmosphere, it is the staff at the Wind Chimes that truly deserves credit. The people at Wind Chimes are friendly and helpful at every moment. They are extremely conscientious and would always provide guidance with places to go, directions to get there, and help you organize your travels. From restaurants to tours, towels to postcards, there was never an unmet need or an unhelpful staff person.From the moment we entered the hotel we felt at ease and at home. They really show you the true meaning of Puerto Rican hospitality.Clearly this is the not the spot to go if you looking for one of the fancy hotels with luxury spotless rooms and a casino in the lobby. However if you are looking to stay at a really convenient place with a wonderful and welcoming staff, a relaxing and refreshing atmosphere, at a very reasonable value, then this is a great place.I know it made our stay in Puerto Rico that much more memorable and enjoyable, and we would definitely stay there again.  
<Date>Jun 27, 2004

<Author>Julieww
<Content>Wonderfully Unique! My husband and I loved this place. It is really nice. The staff was very helpful in answering any questions that we had about the area or meeting our needs with beach towels and letting us keep our luggage there after we checked out and before we needed to be at the airport. They set up a tour guide for us with a wonderful young man, named Hector who did a great job showing us around and was very informative of his native island. He took us to the rainforest which I would recommend to everyone as the sites are beautiful along the way. WindChimes is only a block from the beautiful Condado Beach and the short walk there is through a very nice resisdential neighborhood. It is also in short walking distance to local restaurants (try Bebos for very good Puerto Rician food) and local stores. Back at Wind Chimes you will find a small bar that has great food and drinks. A little expensive but good. The atmosphere is very freindly yet peaceful with security at each door so you feel safe here. It has lots of little terraces and nooks with a real Spanish flavor. The pool is small and has a nice little waterfall in the side center of it. It is quiet and usually no one swimming which made it very nice for my husband and I. I also need to mention that the smell of incense burning in the lobby each day was a nice touch. This place is very clean and comfortable. We will be going back!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Cute Inn, Good Price, Quiet Area Windchimes Inn is a good deal for the price. The Staff is fantastic - friendly, accomodating, and helpful! The boat bar is a nice perk - we had breakfast there every day - very convenient.The room was fine - it was slightly small, and the bathroom shower could've used retiling and a really good scrubbing, but it wasn't that bad. Overall the Inn is very cute, with several nice deck areas and a small pool. It's about a 10 minute walk into Condado - there's a few restaurants, hotel casinos, and bars there. We were there on Thursday and Sunday nights, and there was NO ONE in the bars. In general, we were disappointed with the San Juan nightlife, in Condado AND in Old San Juan. Apparently there are a couple good Techno clubs, but as we don't like Techno we avoided these. Our best evening was at the Parrot Club in Old San Juan - fantastic restaurant with great atmosphere.Windchimes is a short walk to the beach, which is nice. Isla Verde, which is a $10 cab ride has lots of lounge chairs and beach bars/restaurants - a little more going on than the area directly in front of the hotel.We ended up taking taxis a lot, which added up, as we searched for a more lively neighborhood.Basically if you're looking to relax in a reasonably priced, cute place to stay with a fantastic staff, windchimes is your place!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Highly Recommended My wife and I stayed here with friends coming off a week in Mayaguez and then she and I were going on a cruise out of San Juan. We loved this Inn. The staff were so friendly and went the extra mile to work out our requests. We had an unusual parking situation which they bent over backwards to accomodate. We also had laundry we needed cleaned before our cruise and for $20 had everything done by that same afternoon. The Boat Bar was a great place to hang out during the day or evening. It sits in a kind of courtyard area where the seats at the bar are protected but just behind you is open to the sky. We loved sitting there during lunch as it rained for a brief period...very cozy. The food at the bar was good and the drinks excellent. We didn't use the pool as we were not in the mood, but the beach is only a block away and very nice. Our room was large with a king size bed and a nice size bathroom with a large walk-in shower. I noticed a few comments about the hot water, but we had no problem at all taking hot showers. There are a number of nice eating places nearby, from local cuisine to American fare. Shopping is available too within walking distance. We intend to stay here again. It is the perfect place to fly into a few days early before a cruise as it sits between the airport and on the way to the cruise ships. If you have any questions email me at bob007@mac.com.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>An Oasis of Beauty Going to San Juan for an escape from a New York winter, I stumbled upon Wind Chimes. What a marvelous find! First of all, let me say that if you want the Hilton or meaningless glitz, go somewhere else. I happen to love small inns and this one was just marvelous. Yes, the rooms are small, but the whole place is small! Big deal. It is very clean, brightly decorated with original artwork, and the staff is exceptional. It is right on the street, so you do hear traffic, but I live in New York, so that was normal! The Boat Bar, their little bar/restaurant is wonderful - if the weather is bad, or you don't want to go out, you can just eat in. There are all sorts of lovely touches, including that if you want to leave your luggage there after check-out and zip down to the beach, you can do that and then come back for a quick shower before leaving for the airport. The inn is between two strips of fancy hotels, so the beach is less crowded. Bus to Old San Juan is two blocks away, and it's 25c. Is this a five-star hotel? No - but they deserve a 5-star review. I will certainly be going back!  
<Date>Feb 10, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Sometimes you get what you Pay for I just returned from a week's vacation at this guesthouse. When you could find the staff (usually at the bar drinking and smoking) they were helpful, except only the front desk people speak English. I couldn't get the laundry person to understand I wanted a towel to go to the beach. It's a quiet neighborhood area with a few restaurants and the A5 bus to take you into Old San Juan is only a block away. Please be warned, if the sun doesn't shine you will NOT get a hot shower--it's all solar powered. The covered porch is nice, but bring your bug spray--either the mosquito or red ants will have you itching without. They serve food at the bar, but you can't order off the menu--just ask them what they actually have. The tour guide Paul was very friendly and accomodating for including specifics in the tours. He takes you to the place, then someone else does the touring. All in all, I'd say if the weather is nice and you need to save money you could consider Windchimes, but supplement the 3 night minimum with a nicer hotel for the rest of your stay.

<Author>ariel777
<Content>Perfect trip for two kids on a budget! My boyfriend and I stayed in PR for a long Columbus Day weekend vacation. For starters, we would recommend going during the low season- we only paid $75/nigt at our hotel, and $250/each for our round trip flights out of Newark, NJ. The weather was just about perfect (except for 1 day when it rained, and I mean RAINED), and there were just about no tourists swarming through the streets. If we had gone next month (during high season), we would have paid twice as much and been surrounded by tourists. We stayed at Wind Chimes Inn in Condado. EXCELENT hotel, a very quaint boutique hotel. It had some great touches, for example, the lobby always had incense burning, each room (there are only 17 total, I think) was decorated differently, and there's a boat-shaped bar downstairs. Oh, there's also a small lagoon-style pool with a waterfall (!!). The location was perfect, 1 block from the beach, about 2 blocks from the A5 bus stop which drops you right in Old San Juan for a QUARTER, and maybe 5 blocks down to the left of the hotel is the heart of Condado, with tons of casinos and restaurants. It is a residential area, so it feels a bit secluded, but I would rather stay in a quiet neighborhood than in the heart of the city. While you're in PR, make sure you spend at least a full day walking around Old San Juan. Grab a Que Pasa (it's a tourism magazine- they're everywhere) and just rip out the map- it takes a lot of guesswork out of planning a walking tour. While you're in Old San Juan, checl out the African art museum for an amazing mask exhibit, and stop into Nono's for a drink. The Bacardi tour (you have to take a ferry to Catano) is more or less a 2 hour long commercial for Bacardi, but it is interesting, and you get two free Bacardi drinks out of it. One more thing about Condado- try to have dinner at Uvva at Hosteria Del Mar (it's in Ocean Park). The food is the best I've ever had, and they have great vegetarian selections. Another great veg place is Cafe Berlin, in Old San Juan. One thing I can say- we got the BEST tour guide we could ever hope for. His name is Jerry Lowery, and like our hotel, we found him in a user review on TripAdvisor. I researched a lot of different guides, and he was by far the most approachable and flexible, never mind that his rates are a lot less than the bigger tour guides. He is just the friendliest, most capable guide on the whole island. He showed us the island in his open-top Jeep, going kayaking with us in Fajardo's bioluminescent bay (you MUST, MUST do this- it's the most amazing experience in the world) one night, and taking us to El Yunque to swim in La Mina falls the following day. Jerry and I emailed for a few weeks before our plane even landed, so it was more like meeting up with an old friend than a tour guide. Oh, he also knows which roadside restaurants/stands to stop at for a bite (Jerry, if you're reading this, PLEASE send me a pastellillo!!). The time we spent with Jerry were definitely the best parts of our trip. If you're planning a trip, email him at CoquiPIE@aol.com for more info. Anyway, Puerto Rico was a blast. It was the best vacation we'd ever had, and it stayed within our paupers' budget. The people are super friendly, the weather is gorgeous, and the food is insanely good. We're already planning our next trip back, this time for 10 days, not 5.  
<Date>Nov 5, 2003

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A Perfect Oasis We loved this warm and inviting boutique hotel. The location was perfect for a quiet getaway. It is located on the main drag in Condado, just as it changes from the commercial hustle and bustle to the quiet residential area. It is surrounded by beautiful homes on quiet streets. It is about a 10 minute walk to the main commercial area on the strip. Since there are no large public beach parking lots, the stretch of beautiful beach (just a short block away) between Condado proper and Ocean Park Beach is very private and clean.The atmosphere is secluded and intimate. The property is walled and gated with a tropical outdoor bar for guests. My partner and I felt very welcomed and had some wonderful times socializing at the bar with the very friendly and outgoing staff and guests. The homemade food at the bar was very tasty and fresh. The drinks were great! The staff was very helpful in recommending places to eat and see. The private tour guide was terrific and incredibly knowledgeable. He only hosts private tours for individuals, couples, and very small groups and was eager to customize our private tour needs.We stayed in a King room, which was quite roomy and clean. It had a step out balcony with a lovely view of the pool and courtyard. It had a small refrigerator, a futon and a table and chairs. The bed was very comfortable with lots of pillows. The furnishings and artwork were well appointed. The air conditioner was powerful yet quiet. Since we bring our own toiletries when traveling, we didn't mind that the hotel only provides soap and towels.The pool is small but very inviting and refreshing, with its waterfall and water jets. It was fine for a quick dip or short lap or 2. The beach was the place for a real swim.We highly recommend this boutique hotel for its value, convenient and quiet location, peaceful hideaway feeling, intimate atmosphere, and terrific staff. Well be sure to make this our home away from home whenever we visit San Juan.Don't Stay here if you like: being a room number instead of a name, staying in the busiest and noisiest section of town, using a lobby map to navigate your hotel, being re-directed to 2 or 3 people to find and book bus tours on which about 20 or so others will join you, rushing an early breakfast to insure a poolside chair in the sun, an Olympic size pool with an Olympic size crowd, elbow to elbow beach blankets, spending and extra $100 per night for terrycloth robes, a piece of candy on your pillow and a complete line of designer toiletries you should have brought with you.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Beware! READ THIS BEFORE MAKING YOUR RESERVATION !!!!! There is a reason for the variations in reviews for this hotel. Most of it is renovated and quite nice. Several, however, are not renovated. They have tiles peeling up, a stuffy smell and are misrepresented by pictures. If you choose to get a room here, make sure you book it on the phone with a guarantee that it has been renovated. They offered us the unrenovated room for the base price then when we got there tried to get more money out of us to give us a renovated room telling us it was bigger. We didn't need a bigger room, just one that was not misrepresented. This appears to be a scam to get people to pay more than agreed for a room after a long plane ride it is tempting to just pay the extra money and get angry later. Somehow they hide these dingy rooms from the people writing their reviews. Also, they say there is street parking, but you have to walk for blocks to get LEGAL street parking. You may get a ticket, you may not. Hope you like walking a long way to the car.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Awsome! Location a bit secluded... We went to Puerto Rico on vacation druing low season, so the whole island was relatively quiet.l After arriving from the airport to windchimes($15) in less than 10 minutes, we were more than pleasantly suprised by the cute, clean little inn. The rooms were a little small, but the air conditioning was fierce and the beds comfortable. The showers (after hearing how bad the water pressure was) were not the greatest, but the ambiance of the stone cobbled floors and beach-ish feel were so enticing, it overshadowed all flaws in the bathroom. The inn itself is in a quasi-good location. After reading all the reviews we were expecting to be steps from all the Condado action, but soo realized that to get to the main strip, we would have to walk more than the three blocks the front desk told us to, since most of the restaurants and bars we wanted to go to were further down the area. There are a few good options to eat around the area, but everything is mostly residential. Being close to the beach was great though since it was relatively secluded and quiet, however it seemed that the bunch of trees before the beach had some shady behavior going on, as long as your with someone else it should be ok. If one goes straight on the beach, and walks the opposite direction towards ocean park all the way down to the end of the beach(about a 15 minute scenic route) there is a great restaurant overlooking the water that is a real find in a hotel called Hosteria de'l Mer. Also, make sure you take the right bus to Old San Juan, or else you could end up in a really bad area without a clue to get back! Enjoy!!!  
<Date>Sep 10, 2003

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Big disappointment My wife and I recently spent one week in Puerto Rico and very much enjoyed our visit. On our last night we decided to stay at At Wind Chimes Inn since it mostly had good reviews. True, the building looks nice from the outside and even from the inside (for the most part) and the staff is nice, but I began to suspect that something was not quite right when we ran into into mosquito paradise as we where led to our room right above the bar. We accepted the room (big mistake) and dropped off our belongings and off we where to revisit Old San Juan. When we returned later on that evening and entered the room, we were eaten alive by mosquitos to the extent that we called to complain and were given a can of raid! Upon closer inspection, the room had not been dusted in god knows how many years and the floor had not even been mopped, much less swept. The bathroom was no better with broken floor tiles in some parts and large patches of poured concrete in others, plus the tub drain worked only after you finished showering, how nasty! The telephone receiver was full of cerumen and dust and the bedsheets, although supposedly washed, had all sorts of stains on them. To top things off, the room itself had an unforgettable smell and the bed cover was greasy! It was the worst night we've ever spent anywhere, but we couldn't do much about it because we were told earlier that the night staff person had called in sick and there wouldn't be anyone there until 7 am the next morning. We attempted to sleep with the light on thinking that roaches would probalby come out in the dark and left half asleep at 5 am the following day, after my wife refused to use nasty shower. Granted, the photos shown of the room in the brochure look very alluring, but our room was a nightmare! How anyone could recommend this dump or how this place got its high rating is beyond us. I've served in the military for 8 years and I've had to endure some pretty yucky places, but to have to pay for this sort of filth is simply outrageous.

<Content>Would Stay Here Again! Unlike some of the previous reviews I thought this place was great. I stayed here for 5 days and loved every minute of it. Yes the pool is as big as the pool in the marriot but the website clearly showed a complete picture of the pool. I must say that what you see on the website is what you get. The rooms are not big but they are comfortable. I personally could care less about shampoo or soap in the rooms b/c I would bring my own stuff anyway. Besides who wants to use hotel soap anyway... humm. This place was very clean and always cool. They provide you with a ceiling fan and an air conditioner(which is not noisy). My room was located in the courtyard and it was very quiet. The bar is nice and have the best banan margaritas I have ever tasted. The area is quiet and nice. This place is very safe. There is staff around the clock. I would recommend this place to anyone and I would stay here again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Not what we expected After reading the rave reviews, my husband and I expected a lot more from this inn. First the positiives--the inn is a very quaint Spanish villa style with pretty and sunny sitting areas located in a nice section of Condado. The staff are very friendly and the inn, both clean and nicely decorated, is just one block from the beach and convienently located to bus stops. The wraps at the bar are overpriced, yet tasty. However, for more than $100 a night, our room was very tiny and dark, the showers had no water pressure, the three-foot deep pool is super tiny at best, there are little room amenities, and, if your room is located near the bar, be prepared for a lot of noise. It seems that with a few minor upgrades (increase shower water pressure, and provide irons, hairdryers, shampoo, much nicer towels and soap in the rooms, and price differentials for dark rooms--we never knew when it was daylight--) the inn could be a LOT nicer. If you are just looking for a place to sleep on vacation while you explore the city all day, this inn is fine. If you are looking for relaxation in a hotel setting by a decent size pool, pay the extra twenty to thirty dollars and book a room at the major hotels.  
<Date>Apr 26, 2003

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>A disappointment We stayed at the Wind Chimes in April 2003. After reading the reviews in this section we looked forward to a renovated small inn with character and charm. It was far from what we expected. The room and furnishings were dark and unattractive.There was a with noisy wall air conditioner, with no view windows to the outside, on a busy street, small bathroom, shower with low pressure, and no bath amenities except a few bars of thin soap bars.The kitchen facilities were sparse and the few utensiles provided were in a plastic bin.There were no appliances. The inn itself was a maize and reminded us of a european 2 star pensione, (early 1920's style) with little evidence of modernization. In our view it was not worth the $125. per night tarrif.All in all we would not stay there again at any price.
